name: Cost-Savvy Itinerary Planner

code: async def forward(self, taskInfo, extra_info):
    from collections import Counter
    # Initialize sub_tasks and agents lists
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []

    # Sub-task 1: Extract travel parameters
    cot_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Extract travel parameters such as origin, destination cities, dates, and budget from the query."
    cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1([taskInfo], extra_info, cot_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f'Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}')
    agents.append(f'CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, on the purpose of extracting travel parameters, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}')

    # Sub-task 2: Research and select transportation options
    cot_instruction_2 = "Sub-task 2: Based on the outputs from sub-task 1, research and select transportation options between the cities, ensuring they fit within the budget and travel dates."
    N = 5
    cot_agents_2 = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.5) for _ in range(N)]
    thinking_mapping_2 = {}
    answer_mapping_2 = {}
    possible_answers_2 = []
    for i in range(N):
        thinking, answer = await cot_agents_2[i]([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], extra_info, cot_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f'CoT agent {cot_agents_2[i].id}, on the purpose of selecting transportation options, thinking: {thinking.content}; answer: {answer.content}')
        possible_answers_2.append(answer.content)
        thinking_mapping_2[answer.content] = thinking
        answer_mapping_2[answer.content] = answer
    answer2 = Counter(possible_answers_2).most_common(1)[0][0]
    thinking2 = thinking_mapping_2[answer2]
    answer2 = answer_mapping_2[answer2]
    sub_tasks.append(f'Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}')

    # Sub-task 3: Research and select accommodation options
    cot_reflect_instruction_3 = "Sub-task 3: Based on the outputs from sub-task 1, research and select accommodation options for each city, ensuring they fit within the budget and travel dates."
    cot_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_instruction_3 = "Sub-task 3: Based on the outputs from sub-task 1, please review the accommodation selection and provide feedback."
    critic_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_3 = 3
    cot_inputs_3 = [taskInfo, thinking1, answer1]
    thinking3, answer3 = await cot_agent_3(cot_inputs_3, extra_info, cot_reflect_instruction_3, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f'CoT agent {cot_agent_3.id}, on the purpose of selecting accommodations, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}')
    for i in range(N_max_3):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_3([taskInfo, thinking3, answer3], extra_info, critic_instruction_3, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f'Critic agent {critic_agent_3.id}, on the purpose of reviewing accommodations, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}')
        if correct.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs_3.extend([thinking3, answer3, feedback])
        thinking3, answer3 = await cot_agent_3(cot_inputs_3, extra_info, cot_reflect_instruction_3, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f'CoT agent {cot_agent_3.id}, on the purpose of refining accommodations, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}')
    sub_tasks.append(f'Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}')

    # Sub-task 4: Research and select dining options
    cot_instruction_4 = "Sub-task 4: Based on the outputs from sub-task 1, research and select dining options for each day, ensuring they fit within the budget."
    cot_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agent_4([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], extra_info, cot_instruction_4, is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f'Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}')
    agents.append(f'CoT agent {cot_agent_4.id}, on the purpose of selecting dining options, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}')

    # Sub-task 5: Research and select attractions
    debate_instruction_5 = "Sub-task 5: Based on the outputs from sub-task 1, research and select attractions for each city, ensuring they align with the traveler's interests and fit within the budget."
    max_round_5 = 2
    debate_roles_5 = ['Attraction Specialist', 'Budget Analyst']
    debate_agents_5 = [LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Debate Agent', model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.5) for role in debate_roles_5]
    all_thinking_5 = []
    all_answer_5 = []
    for r in range(max_round_5):
        round_thinking = []
        round_answer = []
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_5):
            if r == 0:
                t, a = await agent([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1], extra_info, debate_instruction_5, is_sub_task=True)
                agents.append(f'Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, on the purpose of selecting attractions, thinking: {t.content}; answer: {a.content}')
            else:
                t, a = await agent([taskInfo, thinking1, answer1] + all_thinking_5[r-1], extra_info, debate_instruction_5, is_sub_task=True)
                agents.append(f'Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, on the purpose of refining attractions, thinking: {t.content}; answer: {a.content}')
            round_thinking.append(t)
            round_answer.append(a)
        all_thinking_5.append(round_thinking)
        all_answer_5.append(round_answer)
    final_decision_agent_5 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Final Decision Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking5, answer5 = await final_decision_agent_5(
        [taskInfo] + all_thinking_5[-1] + all_answer_5[-1],
        extra_info,
        "Sub-task 5: Based on the outputs from sub-task 1, finalize the selection of attractions.",
        is_sub_task=True
    )
    agents.append(f'Final Decision agent, on the purpose of finalizing attractions, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}')
    sub_tasks.append(f'Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking5.content}; answer - {answer5.content}')

    # Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.1: Calculate detailed cost breakdown
    cot_instruction_6_4_5_2_2_1 = "Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.1: Calculate the detailed cost breakdown for flights, accommodations, meals, and attractions."
    cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_1 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking6_4_5_2_2_1, answer6_4_5_2_2_1 = await cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_1([taskInfo, thinking2, answer2, thinking3, answer3, thinking4, answer4, thinking5, answer5], extra_info, cot_instruction_6_4_5_2_2_1, is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f'Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.1 output: thinking - {thinking6_4_5_2_2_1.content}; answer - {answer6_4_5_2_2_1.content}')
    agents.append(f'CoT agent {cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_1.id}, on the purpose of calculating cost breakdown, thinking: {thinking6_4_5_2_2_1.content}; answer: {answer6_4_5_2_2_1.content}')

    # Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.2: Identify areas for cost adjustment
    cot_instruction_6_4_5_2_2_2 = "Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.2: Identify areas where cost adjustments are necessary to fit the budget."
    cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_2 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    thinking6_4_5_2_2_2, answer6_4_5_2_2_2 = await cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_2([taskInfo, thinking6_4_5_2_2_1, answer6_4_5_2_2_1], extra_info, cot_instruction_6_4_5_2_2_2, is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f'Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.2 output: thinking - {thinking6_4_5_2_2_2.content}; answer - {answer6_4_5_2_2_2.content}')
    agents.append(f'CoT agent {cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_2.id}, on the purpose of identifying cost adjustments, thinking: {thinking6_4_5_2_2_2.content}; answer: {answer6_4_5_2_2_2.content}')

    # Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.3: Adjust the itinerary based on cost analysis
    cot_reflect_instruction_6_4_5_2_2_3 = "Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.3: Adjust the itinerary based on the cost analysis and ensure it aligns with the budget and preferences. It is known that the previous final responses are incorrect. Ensure the itinerary aligns with the budget and preferences, avoiding known incorrect answers."
    cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_3 = LLMAgentBase(['thinking', 'answer'], 'Chain-of-Thought Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_instruction_6_4_5_2_2_3 = "Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.3: Based on the outputs from sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.2, provide feedback on the final itinerary."
    critic_agent_6_4_5_2_2_3 = LLMAgentBase(['feedback', 'correct'], 'Critic Agent', model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_6_4_5_2_2_3 = 3
    cot_inputs_6_4_5_2_2_3 = [taskInfo, thinking6_4_5_2_2_2, answer6_4_5_2_2_2]
    thinking6_4_5_2_2_3, answer6_4_5_2_2_3 = await cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_3(cot_inputs_6_4_5_2_2_3, extra_info, cot_reflect_instruction_6_4_5_2_2_3, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f'CoT agent {cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_3.id}, on the purpose of finalizing the itinerary, thinking: {thinking6_4_5_2_2_3.content}; answer: {answer6_4_5_2_2_3.content}')
    for i in range(N_max_6_4_5_2_2_3):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_6_4_5_2_2_3([taskInfo, thinking6_4_5_2_2_3, answer6_4_5_2_2_3], extra_info, critic_instruction_6_4_5_2_2_3, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f'Critic agent {critic_agent_6_4_5_2_2_3.id}, on the purpose of reviewing the final itinerary, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}')
        if correct.content == 'True':
            break
        cot_inputs_6_4_5_2_2_3.extend([thinking6_4_5_2_2_3, answer6_4_5_2_2_3, feedback])
        thinking6_4_5_2_2_3, answer6_4_5_2_2_3 = await cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_3(cot_inputs_6_4_5_2_2_3, extra_info, cot_reflect_instruction_6_4_5_2_2_3, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f'CoT agent {cot_agent_6_4_5_2_2_3.id}, on the purpose of refining the final itinerary, thinking: {thinking6_4_5_2_2_3.content}; answer: {answer6_4_5_2_2_3.content}')
    sub_tasks.append(f'Sub-task 6.4.5.2.2.3 output: thinking - {thinking6_4_5_2_2_3.content}; answer - {answer6_4_5_2_2_3.content}')

    # Final answer
    final_answer = self.make_final_answer(thinking6_4_5_2_2_3, answer6_4_5_2_2_3, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer
